# LangChain

Building applications with LLMs through composability

Looking for the JS/TS version? Check out LangChain.js.

**Production Support:** As you move your LangChains into production, we'd love to offer more comprehensive support.

Please fill out this form and we'll set up a dedicated support Slack channel.

## Quick Install

`pip install langchain`

or

`conda install langchain -c conda-forge`

## 🤔 What is this?

Large language models (LLMs) are emerging as a transformative technology, enabling developers to build applications that they previously could not. However, using these LLMs in isolation is often insufficient for creating a truly powerful app - the real power comes when you can combine them with other sources of computation or knowledge.

This library aims to assist in the development of those types of applications. Common examples of these applications include:

**❓ Question Answering over specific documents**

- Documentation

- End-to-end Example: Question Answering over Notion Database

**🤖 Agents**

- Documentation

- End-to-end Example: GPT+WolframAlpha

## 📖 Documentation

Please see [here](https://python.langchain.com) for full documentation on:

- Getting started (installation, setting up the environment, simple examples)

- How-To examples (demos, integrations, helper functions)

- Reference (full API docs)

- Resources (high-level explanation of core concepts)

# AI-Powered Call Center Management Solution

This user manual provides a comprehensive guide to using the AI-powered call center management solution developed in Python. The solution ingests datasets, builds an AI/ML model for actionable insights, and features a basic dashboard with a natural-language query interface.

## Table of Contents

1. [Introduction](#introduction)
2. [Installation Instructions](#installation-instructions)
3. [Main Functions](#main-functions)
4. [How to Use the Software](#how-to-use-the-software)
5. [Troubleshooting](#troubleshooting)

## Introduction

The AI-powered call center management solution is designed to streamline call center operations by leveraging AI and machine learning. The solution includes:

- **Data Ingestion**: Load datasets from various platforms.
- **Model Building**: Train an AI/ML model to generate actionable insights.
- **Dashboard**: A user-friendly interface to visualize insights and recommendations.
- **Natural Language Query Interface**: Allows users to interact with the model using natural language queries.

## Installation Instructions

To set up the environment and install the required dependencies, follow these steps:

1. **Install Python**: Ensure you have Python 3.6 or higher installed on your machine. You can download it from [python.org](https://www.python.org/downloads/).

2. **Install Required Libraries**: Open your terminal or command prompt and run the following command to install the necessary libraries:

   ```bash
   pip install pandas scikit-learn joblib tkinter
   ```

3. **Download the Source Code**: Clone or download the source code files (`main.py`, `data_ingestor.py`, `model_builder.py`, `dashboard.py`, `nl_query.py`) to your local machine.

4. **Prepare Sample Data**: Create a CSV file named `sample_data.csv` in the same directory as the source code. Ensure that the CSV file contains a 'target' column for the model training.

## Main Functions

The solution consists of several key modules:

- **Data Ingestor**: Responsible for loading datasets from CSV files.
- **Model Builder**: Builds and trains a Random Forest Classifier model using the provided data.
- **Dashboard**: Creates a GUI dashboard for displaying insights and recommendations.
- **Natural Language Query**: Processes user queries and provides predictions based on the trained model.

## How to Use the Software

1. **Run the Application**: Navigate to the directory containing the source code files and run the following command:

   ```bash
   python main.py
   ```

2. **Interact with the Dashboard**:
   - A window titled "Call Center Dashboard" will open.
   - You will see a label displaying "Call Center Insights" and an input field for entering queries.
   - Type your natural language query into the input field and click the "Process Query" button.

3. **View Recommendations**: The dashboard will display predictions and insights based on the input query.

## Troubleshooting

- **Error: Target column 'target' not found in the dataset**: Ensure that your CSV file contains a column named 'target'. This column is essential for training the model.

- **No input data provided for prediction**: Make sure that your natural language query can be converted into a suitable input format for the model. You may need to implement the `convert_query_to_input` function in `dashboard.py` to handle specific query formats.

- **GUI Not Opening**: If the dashboard does not appear, ensure that you have installed the `tkinter` library correctly. It is included with standard Python installations, but may require additional steps on some systems.

For further assistance, please contact our support team.

---

This manual provides all the necessary information to install and use the AI-powered call center management solution effectively. Enjoy leveraging AI to enhance your call center operations!
